/*** Add automatic section numbers to headings and table of contents items ***/

#enable-section-numbers {
  display: none;
}

body:has(#enable-section-numbers) {
  #content-area,
  #table-of-contents {
    counter-reset: h2-counter h3-counter h4-counter h5-counter h6-counter;
  }

  #content-area h2[id],
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="0"] {
    counter-set: h3-counter h4-counter h5-counter h6-counter;
  }

  #content-area h3[id],
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="1"] {
    counter-set: h4-counter h5-counter h6-counter;
  }

  #content-area h4[id],
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="2"] {
    counter-set: h5-counter h6-counter;
  }

  #content-area h5[id],
  #content-area h5,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="3"] {
    counter-set: h6-counter;
  }

  #table-of-contents li a::before {
    flex-shrink: 0;
  }

  #content-area h2[id]::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="0"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h2-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) ". ";
  }

  #content-area h3[id]::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="1"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h3-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) "." counter(h3-counter) " ";
  }

  #content-area h4[id]::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="2"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h4-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) "." counter(h3-counter) "." counter(h4-counter)
      " ";
  }

  #content-area h5[id]::before,
  #content-area h5::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="3"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h5-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) "." counter(h3-counter) "." counter(h4-counter)
      "." counter(h5-counter) " ";
  }

  #content-area h6[id]::before,
  #content-area h6::before,
  #table-of-contents li[data-depth="4"] a::before {
    counter-increment: h6-counter;
    content: counter(h2-counter) "." counter(h3-counter) "." counter(h4-counter)
      "." counter(h5-counter) "." counter(h6-counter) " ";
  }
}

  --mt-xl: 1.5rem;

  /* Headings */
  h2, h3 {
    margin: 0;
  }
  .type + h2, .type h3 {
    margin-top: calc(5 * var(--mt-lg));
  }
  h2 + .type h3 {
    margin-top: var(--mt-xl);
  }

  /* Type definition code */
  .tsd-signature {
    margin: var(--mt-lg) 0 0 0;
  }

  /* Prose */
  .tsd-comment {
    margin: var(--mt-lg) 0 0 0;

    p, ul, ol, li {
      margin: 0;
    }

    * + :is(p, ul, ol, pre) {
      margin-top: var(--mt-lg);
    }

    * + li {
      margin-top: var(--mt-sm);
    }
  }

  /* Example block (`@example` tag) */
  .tsd-tag-example {
    margin: var(--mt-lg) 0 0 0;

    summary + * {
      margin: var(--mt-sm) 0 0 0;
      scroll-margin-top: calc(8rem + 1.5rem + var(--mt-sm));
    }
  }

  /* "See" links (`@see` tag) */
  .tsd-tag-see {
    & > :is(p, ul) {
      margin-top: 0;
    }
  }

  /* Type member */
  .tsd-member {
    margin: var(--mt-lg) 0 0 0;

    /* Description */
    .tsd-comment {
      margin-top: var(--mt-sm);
    }

    /* Sub-members */
    .tsd-type-declaration {
      /* List */
      [data-typedoc-h="4"] + .tsd-parameters {
        margin: var(--mt-md) 0 0 0;
      }
    }

    /* Example (`@example` tag) inside type member */
    .tsd-tag-example {
      margin: var(--mt-sm) 0 0 0;
    }
  }
}

body:has(#schema-reference) {
  /* Prose */
  .tsd-comment {
    a.tsd-kind-type-alias,
    a.tsd-kind-interface,
    a.tsd-kind-property {
      font-family: var(--font-mono);
      font-size: 0.875em;
    }
  }

  /* Code blocks */
  .tsd-signature,
  .tsd-tag-example pre:has(code) {
    /* Based on code blocks rendered by Mintlify. */
    border: 1px solid;
    border-color: light-dark(rgb(var(--gray-950)/.1), rgba(255 255 255/0.1));
    border-radius: 1rem;
    padding: 1rem 0.875rem;

    background-color: inherit;
    color: inherit;
    font-family: var(--font-mono);
    font-size: 0.875rem;
    line-height: 1.5rem;
  }

  /* Type definition code */
  .tsd-signature {
    a {
      font-weight: normal;
      border-bottom: none;
      text-decoration: underline;

      &:hover {
        text-decoration-thickness: 2px;
      }
    }

    a[href="#"] {
      pointer-events: none;
      color: inherit;
      text-decoration: none;
    }

    .tsd-signature-keyword {
      color: light-dark(rgb(207, 34, 46), #9CDCFE);
    }

    :is(.tsd-kind-interface, .tsd-kind-type-alias):not(.tsd-signature-type) {
      color: light-dark(rgb(149, 56, 0), #4EC9B0);
    }

    .tsd-signature-type:not(.tsd-kind-interface, .tsd-kind-type-alias) {
      color: light-dark(rgb(5, 80, 174), #DCDCAA);
    }
  }

  /* Example block (`@example` tag) */
  .tsd-tag-example {
    /* Label */
    summary {
      font-weight: 600;
      font-style: italic;
    }

    /* Code */
    pre code.json {
      .hl-1 {
        color: light-dark(rgb(17, 99, 41), #9CDCFE);
      }
      .hl-2, .hl-3 {
        color: light-dark(rgb(10, 48, 105), #CE9178);
      }
      .hl-5 {
        color: light-dark(rgb(5, 80, 174), #569CD6);
      }
    }

    /* Copy button */
    pre button {
      display: none;
    }
  }

  /* "See" links (`@see` tag) */
  .tsd-tag-see {
    /* Add trailing ":" to heading */
    [data-typedoc-h="4"]::after {
      content: ": ";
    }

    /* Hide (defunct) anchor link */
    .tsd-anchor-icon {
      display: none;
    }

    /* Case: single link -- display inline with heading */
    &:has(> p) {
      [data-typedoc-h="4"], p {
        display: inline;
      }
    }
  }

  /* Type member */
  .tsd-member {
    /* Hide members that don't have doc comments */
    &:not(:has(.tsd-comment)) {
      display: none;
    }

    /* When the type itself has a doc comment, add a subtle top border to the first visible member */
    .tsd-comment ~ &:has(.tsd-comment):not(.tsd-member:has(.tsd-comment) ~ *) {
      border-top: 2px solid light-dark(rgb(var(--gray-950)/.05), rgba(255 255 255/0.1));
      padding-top: var(--mt-md);
    }

    /* Member name */
    [data-typedoc-h="3"] {
      font-family: var(--font-mono);
      font-weight: 700;
    }

    & > .tsd-comment,
    & > .tsd-type-declaration {
      margin-left: 1.25rem;
    }

    /* Sub-members */
    .tsd-type-declaration {
      /* Templated heading ("Type Declaration") */
      [data-typedoc-h="4"] {
        display: none;
      }

      /* Name and type */
      [data-typedoc-h="5"] {
        font-family: var(--font-mono);
        font-size: 0.875rem;
        font-weight: 500;

        width: fit-content;
        padding: 0.125em 0.5em;
        background-color: light-dark(rgb(var(--gray-100)/.5), rgb(255 255 255/.05));

        .tsd-tag {
          display: none;
        }
      }
    }

    /* Example (`@example` tag) inside type member */
    .tsd-tag-example {
      padding-left: 0.5rem;
    }

    .tsd-sources {
      display: none;
    }
  }

  /* Anchor links for members and examples */
  .tsd-anchor-icon {
    border: 0;
    padding: 0 0.5rem;
    color: rgb(var(--gray-500)/.5);

    &:hover {
      color: rgb(var(--gray-500))
    }

    &::before {
      content: "#";
      color: inherit;
    }

    svg {
      display: none;
    }
  }

  /* Types with only index properties (e.g., `type Foo = { [key: string]: unknown }`) */
  .type > .tsd-type-declaration {
    /* Hide property if no doc comments */
    &:not(:has(.tsd-comment)) {
      display: none;
    }

    /* Templated heading ("Type Declaration") */
    [data-typedoc-h="4"] {
      display: none;
    }

    /* Index property */
    [data-typedoc-h="5"] {
      font-family: var(--font-mono);
      font-weight: 700;
    }
  }
}

0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Introduction</span></h2>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="purpose-and-scope"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#purpose-and-scope" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Purpose and Scope</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">This document provides security considerations for the Model Context
Protocol (MCP), complementing the
<a class="link" href="/specification/latest/basic/authorization">MCP Authorization</a>
specification. This document identifies security risks, attack vectors,
and best practices specific to MCP implementations.</span>
<span data-as="p">The primary audience for this document includes developers implementing
MCP authorization flows, MCP server operators, and security
professionals evaluating MCP-based systems. This document should be read
alongside the MCP Authorization specification and
<a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc9700" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">OAuth 2.0 security best practices</a>.</span>
<h2 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="attacks-and-mitigations"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#attacks-and-mitigations" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Attacks and Mitigations</span></h2>
<span data-as="p">This section gives a detailed description of attacks on MCP
implementations, along with potential countermeasures.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="confused-deputy-problem"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#confused-deputy-problem" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Confused Deputy Problem</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Attackers can exploit MCP proxy servers that connect to third-party
APIs, creating
“<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Confused_deputy_problem" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">confused deputy</a>”
vulnerabilities. This attack allows malicious clients to obtain
authorization codes without proper user consent by exploiting the
combination of static client IDs, dynamic client registration, and
consent cookies.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="terminology"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#terminology" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Terminology</span></h4>
<span data-as="p"><strong>MCP Proxy Server</strong>
: An MCP server that connects MCP clients to third-party APIs, offering
MCP features while delegating operations and acting as a single OAuth
client to the third-party API server.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Third-Party Authorization Server</strong>
: Authorization server that protects the third-party API. It may lack
dynamic client registration support, requiring the MCP proxy to use a
static client ID for all requests.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Third-Party API</strong>
: The protected resource server that provides the actual API
functionality. Access to this API requires tokens issued by the
third-party authorization server.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Static Client ID</strong>
: A fixed OAuth 2.0 client identifier used by the MCP proxy server when
communicating with the third-party authorization server. This Client ID
refers to the MCP server acting as a client to the Third-Party API. It
is the same value for all MCP server to Third-Party API interactions
regardless of which MCP client initiated the request.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="vulnerable-conditions"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#vulnerable-conditions" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Vulnerable Conditions</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">This attack becomes possible when all of the following conditions are
present:</span>
<ul>
<li>MCP proxy server uses a <strong>static client ID</strong> with a third-party
authorization server</li>
<li>MCP proxy server allows MCP clients to <strong>dynamically register</strong> (each
getting their own client_id)</li>
<li>The third-party authorization server sets a <strong>consent cookie</strong> after
the first authorization</li>
<li>MCP proxy server does not implement proper per-client consent before
forwarding to third-party authorization</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="architecture-and-attack-flows"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#architecture-and-attack-flows" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Architecture and Attack Flows</span></h4>
<h5>Normal OAuth proxy usage (preserves user consent)</h5>
<!--$!--><template data-dgst="BAILOUT_TO_CLIENT_SIDE_RENDERING"></template><!--/$-->
<h5>Malicious OAuth proxy usage (skips user consent)</h5>
<!--$!--><template data-dgst="BAILOUT_TO_CLIENT_SIDE_RENDERING"></template><!--/$-->
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="attack-description"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#attack-description" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Attack Description</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">When an MCP proxy server uses a static client ID to authenticate with
a third-party authorization server, the following attack becomes
possible:</span>
<ol>
<li>A user authenticates normally through the MCP proxy server to access
the third-party API</li>
<li>During this flow, the third-party authorization server sets a cookie
on the user agent indicating consent for the static client ID</li>
<li>An attacker later sends the user a malicious link containing a
crafted authorization request which contains a malicious redirect URI
along with a new dynamically registered client ID</li>
<li>When the user clicks the link, their browser still has the consent
cookie from the previous legitimate request</li>
<li>The third-party authorization server detects the cookie and skips the
consent screen</li>
<li>The MCP authorization code is redirected to the attacker’s server
(specified in the malicious <code>redirect_uri</code> parameter during
<a class="link" href="/specification/latest/basic/authorization#dynamic-client-registration">dynamic client registration</a>)</li>
<li>The attacker exchanges the stolen authorization code for access
tokens for the MCP server without the user’s explicit approval</li>
<li>The attacker now has access to the third-party API as the compromised
user</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="mitigation"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#mitigation" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Mitigation</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">To prevent confused deputy attacks, MCP proxy servers <strong>MUST</strong> implement
per-client consent and proper security controls as detailed below.</span>
<h5>Consent Flow Implementation</h5>
<span data-as="p">The following diagram shows how to properly implement per-client consent
that runs <strong>before</strong> the third-party authorization flow:</span>
<!--$!--><template data-dgst="BAILOUT_TO_CLIENT_SIDE_RENDERING"></template><!--/$-->
<h5>Required Protections</h5>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Per-Client Consent Storage</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">MCP proxy servers <strong>MUST</strong>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Maintain a registry of approved <code>client_id</code> values per user</li>
<li>Check this registry <strong>before</strong> initiating the third-party
authorization flow</li>
<li>Store consent decisions securely (server-side database, or server
specific cookies)</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Consent UI Requirements</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">The MCP-level consent page <strong>MUST</strong>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Clearly identify the requesting MCP client by name</li>
<li>Display the specific third-party API scopes being requested</li>
<li>Show the registered <code>redirect_uri</code> where tokens will be sent</li>
<li>Implement CSRF protection (e.g., state parameter, CSRF tokens)</li>
<li>Prevent iframing via <code>frame-ancestors</code> CSP directive or
<code>X-Frame-Options: DENY</code> to prevent clickjacking</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Consent Cookie Security</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">If using cookies to track consent decisions, they <strong>MUST</strong>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Use <code>__Host-</code> prefix for cookie names</li>
<li>Set <code>Secure</code>, <code>HttpOnly</code>, and <code>SameSite=Lax</code> attributes</li>
<li>Be cryptographically signed or use server-side sessions</li>
<li>Bind to the specific <code>client_id</code> (not just “user has consented”)</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Redirect URI Validation</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">The MCP proxy server <strong>MUST</strong>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Validate that the <code>redirect_uri</code> in authorization requests exactly
matches the registered URI</li>
<li>Reject requests if the <code>redirect_uri</code> has changed without
re-registration</li>
<li>Use exact string matching (not pattern matching or wildcards)</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>OAuth State Parameter Validation</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">The OAuth <code>state</code> parameter is critical to prevent authorization code
interception and CSRF attacks. Proper state validation ensures that
consent approval at the authorization endpoint is enforced at the
callback endpoint.</span>
<span data-as="p">MCP proxy servers implementing OAuth flows <strong>MUST</strong>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Generate a cryptographically secure random <code>state</code> value for each
authorization request</li>
<li>Store the <code>state</code> value server-side (in a secure session store or
encrypted cookie) <strong>only after</strong> consent has been explicitly approved</li>
<li>Set the <code>state</code> tracking cookie/session <strong>immediately before</strong>
redirecting to the third-party identity provider (not before consent
approval)</li>
<li>Validate at the callback endpoint that the <code>state</code> query parameter
exactly matches the stored value in the callback request’s cookies or
in the request’s cookie-based session</li>
<li>Reject any callback requests where the <code>state</code> parameter is missing
or does not match</li>
<li>Ensure <code>state</code> values are single-use (delete after validation) and
have a short expiration time (e.g., 10 minutes)</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p">The consent cookie or session containing the <code>state</code> value <strong>MUST NOT</strong>
be set until <strong>after</strong> the user has approved the consent screen at the
MCP server’s authorization endpoint. Setting this cookie before consent
approval renders the consent screen ineffective, as an attacker could
bypass it by crafting a malicious authorization request.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="token-passthrough"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#token-passthrough" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Token Passthrough</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">“Token passthrough” is an anti-pattern where an MCP server accepts
tokens from an MCP client without validating that the tokens were
properly issued <em>to the MCP server</em> and passes them through to the
downstream API.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="risks"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#risks" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Risks</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">Token passthrough is explicitly forbidden in the
<a class="link" href="/specification/latest/basic/authorization">authorization specification</a>
as it introduces a number of security risks, that include:</span>
<ul>
<li><strong>Security Control Circumvention</strong>
<ul>
<li>The MCP Server or downstream APIs might implement important security
controls like rate limiting, request validation, or traffic
monitoring, that depend on the token audience or other credential
constraints. If clients can obtain and use tokens directly with the
downstream APIs without the MCP server validating them properly or
ensuring that the tokens are issued for the right service, they
bypass these controls.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Accountability and Audit Trail Issues</strong>
<ul>
<li>The MCP Server will be unable to identify or distinguish between MCP
Clients when clients are calling with an upstream-issued access token
which may be opaque to the MCP Server.</li>
<li>The downstream Resource Server’s logs may show requests that appear
to come from a different source with a different identity, rather
than the MCP server that is actually forwarding the tokens.</li>
<li>Both factors make incident investigation, controls, and auditing
more difficult.</li>
<li>If the MCP Server passes tokens without validating their claims
(e.g., roles, privileges, or audience) or other metadata, a
malicious actor in possession of a stolen token can use the server
as a proxy for data exfiltration.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Trust Boundary Issues</strong>
<ul>
<li>The downstream Resource Server grants trust to specific entities.
This trust might include assumptions about origin or client behavior
patterns. Breaking this trust boundary could lead to unexpected
issues.</li>
<li>If the token is accepted by multiple services without proper
validation, an attacker compromising one service can use the token
to access other connected services.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>Future Compatibility Risk</strong>
<ul>
<li>Even if an MCP Server starts as a “pure proxy” today, it might need
to add security controls later. Starting with proper token audience
separation makes it easier to evolve the security model.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="mitigation-2"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#mitigation-2" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Mitigation</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">MCP servers <strong>MUST NOT</strong> accept any tokens that were not explicitly
issued for the MCP server.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="server-side-request-forgery-ssrf"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#server-side-request-forgery-ssrf" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Server-Side Request Forgery (SSRF)</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Server-Side Request Forgery (SSRF) is an attack where an attacker can
induce an MCP client to make HTTP requests to unintended destinations,
potentially accessing internal network resources, cloud metadata
endpoints, or other protected services.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="attack-description-2"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#attack-description-2" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Attack Description</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">During OAuth metadata discovery, MCP clients fetch URLs from several
sources that could be controlled by a malicious MCP server:</span>
<ol>
<li>The <code>resource_metadata</code> URL from the <code>WWW-Authenticate</code> header</li>
<li>The <code>authorization_servers</code> URLs from the Protected Resource Metadata
document</li>
<li>The <code>token_endpoint</code>, <code>authorization_endpoint</code>, and other URLs from
Authorization Server Metadata</li>
</ol>
<span data-as="p">A malicious MCP server can populate these fields with URLs pointing to
internal resources, enabling the following attack patterns:</span>
<ul>
<li><strong>Direct internal IP access</strong>: URLs like <code>http://192.168.1.1/admin</code> or
<code>http://10.0.0.1/api</code> target internal network services</li>
<li><strong>Cloud metadata endpoints</strong>: URLs targeting
<code>http://169.254.169.254/</code> (AWS/GCP/Azure metadata service) can
exfiltrate cloud credentials and instance information</li>
<li><strong>Localhost services</strong>: URLs like <code>http://localhost:6379/</code> can interact
with local services (Redis, databases, admin panels)</li>
<li><strong>DNS rebinding</strong>: Domains that change DNS resolution between
validation and use (e.g., <code>https://attacker.com</code> resolving to a safe
IP initially, then to <code>192.168.1.1</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Redirect chains</strong>: Normal-looking URLs that redirect to internal
resources</li>
</ul>
<!--$!--><template data-dgst="BAILOUT_TO_CLIENT_SIDE_RENDERING"></template><!--/$-->
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="risks-2"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#risks-2" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Risks</span></h4>
<ul>
<li><strong>Credential exfiltration</strong>: Cloud metadata endpoints often expose
IAM credentials, API keys, and other secrets</li>
<li><strong>Internal network reconnaissance</strong>: Error messages reveal information
about internal network topology and services</li>
<li><strong>Service interaction</strong>: POST requests (e.g., to token endpoints) can
trigger mutations on internal services</li>
<li><strong>Firewall bypass</strong>: The MCP client acts as a proxy, bypassing network
perimeter controls</li>
<li><strong>Data exfiltration</strong>: Internal service responses may be reflected back
to attackers through error messages or OAuth flows</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="mitigation-3"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#mitigation-3" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Mitigation</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">MCP clients deployed to a server <strong>MUST</strong> consider SSRF risks and
implement appropriate mitigations when fetching OAuth-related URLs.
Which protections are appropriate depend on your network environment.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Enforce HTTPS</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">MCP clients <strong>SHOULD</strong> require HTTPS for all OAuth-related URLs in
production environments:</span>
<ul>
<li>Reject <code>http://</code> URLs except for loopback addresses (<code>localhost</code>,
<code>127.0.0.1</code>, <code>::1</code>) during development</li>
<li>This aligns with
<a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/draft-ietf-oauth-v2-1-13#section-1.5" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">OAuth 2.1 Section 1.5</a>
which requires HTTPS for all OAuth protocol URLs except loopback
redirect URIs</li>
<li>Provide an explicit opt-out mechanism for development/testing
scenarios</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Block Private IP Ranges</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">MCP clients <strong>SHOULD</strong> block requests to private and reserved IP address
ranges as recommended by
<a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc9728#section-7.7" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">RFC 9728 Section 7.7</a>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Private IPv4 ranges: <code>10.0.0.0/8</code>, <code>172.16.0.0/12</code>,
<code>192.168.0.0/16</code></li>
<li>Loopback: <code>127.0.0.0/8</code>, <code>::1</code> (except when explicitly allowed for
development)</li>
<li>Link-local: <code>169.254.0.0/16</code> (including cloud metadata endpoints)</li>
<li>Private IPv6 ranges: <code>fc00::/7</code>, <code>fe80::/10</code></li>
</ul>
<div class="callout my-4 px-5 py-4 overflow-hidden rounded-2xl flex gap-3 border border-blue-200 bg-blue-50 dark:border-blue-900 dark:bg-blue-600/20" data-callout-type="note"><div class="mt-0.5 w-4" data-component-part="callout-icon"><svg width="14" height="14" viewBox="0 0 14 14" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="size-4 text-blue-800 dark:text-blue-300" aria-label="Note"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M7 1.3C10.14 1.3 12.7 3.86 12.7 7C12.7 10.14 10.14 12.7 7 12.7C5.48908 12.6974 4.0408 12.096 2.97241 11.0276C1.90403 9.9592 1.30264 8.51092 1.3 7C1.3 3.86 3.86 1.3 7 1.3ZM7 0C3.14 0 0 3.14 0 7C0 10.86 3.14 14 7 14C10.86 14 14 10.86 14 7C14 3.14 10.86 0 7 0ZM8 3H6V8H8V3ZM8 9H6V11H8V9Z"></path></svg></div><div class="text-sm prose dark:prose-invert min-w-0 w-full [&amp;_kbd]:bg-background-light dark:[&amp;_kbd]:bg-background-dark [&amp;_code]:!text-current [&amp;_kbd]:!text-current [&amp;_a]:!text-current [&amp;_a]:border-current [&amp;_strong]:!text-current text-blue-800 dark:text-blue-300" data-component-part="callout-content"><span data-as="p">Avoid implementing IP validation manually. Attackers exploit encoding tricks
(octal, hex, IPv4-mapped IPv6) that custom parsers often miss.</span></div></div>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Validate Redirect Targets</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">MCP clients <strong>SHOULD</strong> apply the same URL validation to redirect
targets:</span>
<ul>
<li>Do not blindly follow redirects to internal resources</li>
<li>Apply HTTPS and IP range restrictions to redirect destinations</li>
<li>Consider disabling automatic redirect following and validating each
hop</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Use Egress Proxies</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">For server-side MCP client deployments, operators <strong>SHOULD</strong> consider
using an egress proxy that enforces network policies:</span>
<ul>
<li>Route OAuth discovery requests through a proxy that blocks internal
destinations</li>
<li>Use tools like
<a href="https://github.com/stripe/smokescreen" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">Smokescreen</a> or similar
egress proxies that prevent SSRF by design</li>
<li>Configure network policies to restrict the MCP client’s outbound
access</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p"><strong>DNS Resolution Considerations</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">Be aware of Time-of-Check to Time-of-Use (TOCTOU) issues with
DNS-based validation:</span>
<ul>
<li>An attacker’s domain may resolve to a safe IP during validation but
to an internal IP during the actual request</li>
<li>Consider pinning DNS resolution results between check and use</li>
<li>Defense in depth: combine DNS checks with other mitigations</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="resources-and-tools"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#resources-and-tools" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Resources and Tools</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">The following resources can help developers implement SSRF protections
in MCP clients.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Reference Documentation</strong></span>
<ul>
<li><a href="https://cheatsheetseries.owasp.org/cheatsheets/Server_Side_Request_Forgery_Prevention_Cheat_Sheet.html" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">OWASP SSRF Prevention Cheat Sheet</a>:
Comprehensive guidance on SSRF prevention techniques, including input
validation, allowlist strategies, and network-level controls</li>
<li><a href="https://owasp.org/Top10/2021/A10_2021-Server-Side_Request_Forgery_%28SSRF%29/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer" class="link">OWASP Top 10 A10:2021 - SSRF</a>:
SSRF in the context of the most critical web application security
risks</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="session-hijacking"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#session-hijacking" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Session Hijacking</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Session hijacking is an attack vector where a client is provided a
session ID by the server, and an unauthorized party is able to obtain
and use that same session ID to impersonate the original client and
perform unauthorized actions on their behalf.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="session-hijack-prompt-injection"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#session-hijack-prompt-injection" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Session Hijack Prompt Injection</span></h4>
<!--$!--><template data-dgst="BAILOUT_TO_CLIENT_SIDE_RENDERING"></template><!--/$-->
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="session-hijack-impersonation"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#session-hijack-impersonation" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Session Hijack Impersonation</span></h4>
<!--$!--><template data-dgst="BAILOUT_TO_CLIENT_SIDE_RENDERING"></template><!--/$-->
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="attack-description-3"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#attack-description-3" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Attack Description</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">When you have multiple stateful HTTP servers that handle MCP requests,
the following attack vectors are possible:</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Session Hijack Prompt Injection</strong></span>
<ol>
<li>
<span data-as="p">The client connects to <strong>Server A</strong> and receives a session ID.</span>
</li>
<li>
<span data-as="p">The attacker obtains an existing session ID and sends a malicious
event to <strong>Server B</strong> with said session ID.</span>
<ul>
<li>When a server supports
<a class="link" href="/specification/latest/basic/transports#resumability-and-redelivery">redelivery/resumable streams</a>,
deliberately terminating the request before receiving the response
could lead to it being resumed by the original client via the GET
request for server sent events.</li>
<li>If a particular server initiates server sent events as a
consequence of a tool call such as a
<code>notifications/tools/list_changed</code>, where it is possible to affect
the tools that are offered by the server, a client could end up
with tools that they were not aware were enabled.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Server B</strong> enqueues the event (associated with session ID) into a
shared queue.</span>
</li>
<li>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Server A</strong> polls the queue for events using the session ID and
retrieves the malicious payload.</span>
</li>
<li>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Server A</strong> sends the malicious payload to the client as an
asynchronous or resumed response.</span>
</li>
<li>
<span data-as="p">The client receives and acts on the malicious payload, leading to
potential compromise.</span>
</li>
</ol>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Session Hijack Impersonation</strong></span>
<ol>
<li>The MCP client authenticates with the MCP server, creating a
persistent session ID.</li>
<li>The attacker obtains the session ID.</li>
<li>The attacker makes calls to the MCP server using the session ID.</li>
<li>MCP server does not check for additional authorization and treats the
attacker as a legitimate user, allowing unauthorized access or
actions.</li>
</ol>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="mitigation-4"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#mitigation-4" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Mitigation</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">To prevent session hijacking and event injection attacks, the following
mitigations should be implemented:</span>
<span data-as="p">MCP servers that implement authorization <strong>MUST</strong> verify all inbound
requests. MCP Servers <strong>MUST NOT</strong> use sessions for authentication.</span>
<span data-as="p">MCP servers <strong>MUST</strong> use secure, non-deterministic session IDs.
Generated session IDs (e.g., UUIDs) <strong>SHOULD</strong> use secure random number
generators. Avoid predictable or sequential session identifiers that
could be guessed by an attacker. Rotating or expiring session IDs can
also reduce the risk.</span>
<span data-as="p">MCP servers <strong>SHOULD</strong> bind session IDs to user-specific information.
When storing or transmitting session-related data (e.g., in a queue),
combine the session ID with information unique to the authorized user,
such as their internal user ID. Use a key format like
<code>&lt;user_id&gt;:&lt;session_id&gt;</code>. This ensures that even if an attacker guesses
a session ID, they cannot impersonate another user as the user ID is
derived from the user token and not provided by the client.</span>
<span data-as="p">MCP servers can optionally leverage additional unique identifiers.</span>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="local-mcp-server-compromise"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#local-mcp-server-compromise" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Local MCP Server Compromise</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Local MCP servers are MCP Servers running on a user’s local machine,
either by the user downloading and executing a server, authoring a
server themselves, or installing through a client’s configuration flows.
These servers may have direct access to the user’s system and may be
accessible to other processes running on the user’s machine, making them
attractive targets for attacks.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="attack-description-4"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#attack-description-4" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Attack Description</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">Local MCP servers are binaries that are downloaded and executed on the
same machine as the MCP client. Without proper sandboxing and consent
requirements in place, the following attacks become possible:</span>
<ol>
<li>An attacker includes a malicious “startup” command in a client
configuration</li>
<li>An attacker distributes a malicious payload inside the server itself</li>
<li>An attacker accesses an insecure local server that’s left running on
localhost via DNS rebinding</li>
</ol>
<span data-as="p">Example malicious startup commands that could be embedded:</span>
<div class="code-block mt-5 mb-8 not-prose rounded-2xl relative group text-gray-950 dark:text-gray-50 codeblock-light border border-gray-950/10 dark:border-white/10 dark:twoslash-dark bg-transparent dark:bg-transparent" numberOfLines="5" language="shellscript"><div data-floating-buttons="true" class="absolute top-3 right-4 flex items-center gap-1.5"><div class="z-10 relative select-none"><button text-tooltip-foreground rounded-lg px-1.5 py-0.5 text-xs bg-primary-dark">Copy</div></div></div><div class="w-0 min-w-full max-w-full py-3.5 px-4 h-full dark:bg-codeblock relative text-sm leading-6 children:!my-0 children:!shadow-none children:!bg-transparent transition-[height] duration-300 ease-in-out code-block-background [&amp;_*]:ring-0 [&amp;_*]:outline-0 [&amp;_*]:focus:ring-0 [&amp;_*]:focus:outline-0 rounded-2xl bg-white overflow-x-auto scrollbar-thin scrollbar-thumb-rounded scrollbar-thumb-black/15 hover:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 active:scrollbar-thumb-black/20 dark:scrollbar-thumb-white/20 dark:hover:scrollbar-thumb-white/25 dark:active:scrollbar-thumb-white/25" data-component-part="code-block-root" tabindex="0" style="font-variant-ligatures:none;height:auto;background-color:#ffffff;--shiki-dark-bg:#0B0C0E"><div class="font-mono whitespace-pre leading-6"><pre class="shiki shiki-themes github-light-default
