<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#6E7781;--shiki-dark:#6A9955"># Privilege escalation</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#953800;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">sudo</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> rm</span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#569CD6"> -rf</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> /important/system/files</span><span style="color:#1F2328;--shiki-dark:#D4D4D4"> &amp;&amp; </span><span style="color:#0550AE;--shiki-dark:#DCDCAA">echo</span><span style="color:#0A3069;--shiki-dark:#CE9178"> &quot;MCP server installed!&quot;</span></span>
</code></pre></div></div><div data-fade-overlay="true" aria-hidden="true" style="--fade-color-light:#ffffff;--fade-color-dark:#0B0C0E"></div></div>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="risks-3"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#risks-3" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Risks</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">Local MCP servers with inadequate restrictions or from untrusted sources
introduce several critical security risks:</span>
<ul>
<li><strong>Arbitrary code execution</strong>. Attackers can execute any command with
MCP client privileges.</li>
<li><strong>No visibility</strong>. Users have no insight into what commands are being
executed.</li>
<li><strong>Command obfuscation</strong>. Malicious actors can use complex or
convoluted commands to appear legitimate.</li>
<li><strong>Data exfiltration</strong>. Attackers can access legitimate local MCP
servers via compromised JavaScript.</li>
<li><strong>Data loss</strong>. Attackers or bugs in legitimate servers could lead to
irrecoverable data loss on the host machine.</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="mitigation-5"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#mitigation-5" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Mitigation</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">If an MCP client supports one-click local MCP server configuration, it
<strong>MUST</strong> implement proper consent mechanisms prior to executing commands.</span>
<span data-as="p"><strong>Pre-Configuration Consent</strong></span>
<span data-as="p">Display a clear consent dialog before connecting a new local MCP server
via one-click configuration. The MCP client <strong>MUST</strong>:</span>
<ul>
<li>Show the exact command that will be executed, without truncation
(include arguments and parameters)</li>
<li>Clearly identify it as a potentially dangerous operation that executes
code on the user’s system</li>
<li>Require explicit user approval before proceeding</li>
<li>Allow users to cancel the configuration</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p">The MCP client <strong>SHOULD</strong> implement additional checks and guardrails to
mitigate potential code execution attack vectors:</span>
<ul>
<li>Highlight potentially dangerous command patterns (e.g., commands
containing <code>sudo</code>, <code>rm -rf</code>, network operations, file system access
outside expected directories)</li>
<li>Display warnings for commands that access sensitive locations (home
directory, SSH keys, system directories)</li>
<li>Warn that MCP servers run with the same privileges as the client</li>
<li>Execute MCP server commands in a sandboxed environment with minimal
default privileges</li>
<li>Launch MCP servers with restricted access to the file system, network,
and other system resources</li>
<li>Provide mechanisms for users to explicitly grant additional privileges
(e.g., specific directory access, network access) when needed</li>
<li>Use platform-appropriate sandboxing technologies (containers, chroot,
application sandboxes, etc.)</li>
<li>Keep sandboxing solutions up-to-date to account for emerging
vulnerabilities</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p">MCP servers intending for their servers to be run locally <strong>SHOULD</strong>
implement measures to prevent unauthorized usage from malicious
processes:</span>
<ul>
<li>Use the <code>stdio</code> transport to limit access to just the MCP client</li>
<li>Restrict access if using an HTTP transport, such as:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li>Require an authorization token</li>
<li>Use unix domain sockets or other Interprocess Communication (IPC)
mechanisms with restricted access</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="scope-minimization"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#scope-minimization" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Scope Minimization</span></h3>
<span data-as="p">Poor scope design increases token compromise impact, elevates user
friction, and obscures audit trails.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="attack-description-5"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#attack-description-5" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Attack Description</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">An attacker obtains (via log leakage, memory scraping, or local
interception) an access token carrying broad scopes (<code>files:*</code>, <code>db:*</code>,
<code>admin:*</code>) that were granted up front because the MCP server exposed
every scope in <code>scopes_supported</code> and the client requested them all.
The token enables lateral data access, privilege chaining, and difficult
revocation without re-consenting the entire surface.</span>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="risks-4"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#risks-4" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Risks</span></h4>
<ul>
<li>Expanded blast radius: stolen broad token enables unrelated
tool/resource access</li>
<li>Higher friction on revocation: revoking a max-privilege token disrupts
all workflows</li>
<li>Audit noise: single omnibus scope masks user intent per operation</li>
<li>Privilege chaining: attacker can immediately invoke high-risk tools
without further elevation prompts</li>
<li>Consent abandonment: users decline dialogs listing excessive scopes</li>
<li>Scope inflation blindness: lack of metrics makes over-broad requests
normalised</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="mitigation-6"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#mitigation-6" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Mitigation</span></h4>
<span data-as="p">Implement a progressive, least-privilege scope model:</span>
<ul>
<li>Minimal initial scope set (e.g., <code>mcp:tools-basic</code>) containing only
low-risk discovery/read operations</li>
<li>Incremental elevation via targeted <code>WWW-Authenticate</code> <code>scope=&quot;...&quot;</code>
challenges when privileged operations are first attempted</li>
<li>Down-scoping tolerance: server should accept reduced scope tokens;
auth server MAY issue a subset of requested scopes</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p">Server guidance:</span>
<ul>
<li>Emit precise scope challenges; avoid returning the full catalog</li>
<li>Log elevation events (scope requested, granted subset) with
correlation IDs</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p">Client guidance:</span>
<ul>
<li>Begin with only baseline scopes (or those specified by initial
<code>WWW-Authenticate</code>)</li>
<li>Cache recent failures to avoid repeated elevation loops for denied
scopes</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="flex whitespace-pre-wrap group font-semibold" id="common-mistakes"><div class="absolute" tabindex="-1"><a href="#common-mistakes" class="-ml-10 flex items-center opacity-0 border-0 group-hover:opacity-100 focus:opacity-100 focus:outline-0 group/link" aria-label="Navigate to header">​<div class="w-6 h-6 rounded-md flex items-center justify-center shadow-sm text-gray-400 dark:text-white/50 dark:bg-background-dark dark:brightness-[1.35] dark:ring-1 dark:hover:brightness-150 bg-white ring-1 ring-gray-400/30 dark:ring-gray-700/25 hover:ring-gray-400/60 dark:hover:ring-white/20 group-focus/link:border-2 group-focus/link:border-primary dark:group-focus/link:border-primary-light"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="gray" height="12px" viewBox="0 0 576 512"><path d="M0 256C0 167.6 71.6 96 160 96h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C98.1 144 48 194.1 48 256s50.1 112 112 112h72c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H160C71.6 416 0 344.4 0 256zm576 0c0 88.4-71.6 160-160 160H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c61.9 0 112-50.1 112-112s-50.1-112-112-112H344c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24h72c88.4 0 160 71.6 160 160zM184 232H392c13.3 0 24 10.7 24 24s-10.7 24-24 24H184c-13.3 0-24-10.7-24-24s10.7-24 24-24z"></path></svg></div></a></div><span class="cursor-pointer">Common Mistakes</span></h4>
<ul>
<li>Publishing all possible scopes in <code>scopes_supported</code></li>
<li>Using wildcard or omnibus scopes (<code>*</code>, <code>all</code>, <code>full-access</code>)</li>
<li>Bundling unrelated privileges to preempt future prompts</li>
<li>Returning entire scope catalog in every challenge</li>
<li>Silent scope semantic changes without versioning</li>
<li>Treating claimed scopes in token as sufficient without server-side
authorization logic</li>
</ul>
<span data-as="p">Proper minimization constrains compromise impact, improves audit
clarity, and reduces consent churn.</span></div><div class="feedback-toolbar pb-16 w-full flex flex-col gap-y-8"><div class="flex flex-row flex-wrap gap-4 items-center justify-between"><p class="inline-block text-sm text-gray-600 dark:text-gray-400 whitespace-nowrap">Was this page helpful?</p><div class="flex flex-wrap flex-grow gap-3 items-center justify-end"><div class="flex gap-3 Attacker impersonates user to MCP server\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"attack-description\",\n      children: \"Attack Description\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: \"When an MCP proxy server uses a static client ID to authenticate with\\na third-party authorization server, the following attack becomes\\npossible:\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ol, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"A user authenticates normally through the MCP proxy server to access\\nthe third-party API\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"During this flow, the third-party authorization server sets a cookie\\non the user agent indicating consent for the static client ID\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"An attacker later sends the user a malicious link containing a\\ncrafted authorization request which contains a malicious redirect URI\\nalong with a new dynamically registered client ID\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"When the user clicks the link, their browser still has the consent\\ncookie from the previous legitimate request\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"The third-party authorization server detects the cookie and skips the\\nconsent screen\"\n      }), client registration\"\n        }), \")\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"The attacker exchanges the stolen authorization code for access\\ntokens for the MCP server without the user’s explicit approval\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"The attacker now has access to the third-party API as the compromised\\nuser\"\n      }), \"\\n\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"mitigation\",\n      children: \"Mitigation\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"To prevent   }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.h5, {\n      children: \"Consent Flow Implementation\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"The following diagram shows how to properly chart: \"sequenceDiagram\\n    participant Client as MCP Client\\n    participant Browser as User's Browser\\n    participant MCP as MCP Server\\n    participant ThirdParty as Third-Party AuthZ Server\\n\\n    Note over Client,ThirdParty: 1. Client Registration (Dynamic)\\n    Client-\u003e\u003eMCP: Register with redirect_uri\\n    MCP--\u003e\u003eClient: client_id\\n\\n    Note over Client,ThirdParty: 2. registered redirect_uri\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.h5, {\n      children: \"Required Protections\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: _jsx(_components.strong, {\n children: [\"The MCP proxy server \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"MUST\"\n      }), \":\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"OAuth State Parameter Validation\"\n      })\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"The OAuth \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n        children: \"state\"\n      }), \" parameter is critical to prevent authorization code\\ninterception and CSRF attacks. {\n        children: [\"Generate a cryptographically secure random \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"state\"\n        }), \" value for each\\nauthorization request\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"Store the \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"state\"\n        }), \" value server-side (in a secure session store or\\nencrypted session\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"Reject any callback requests where the \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"state\"\n        }), \" Setting this cookie before consent\\napproval renders the consent screen ineffective, as an attacker could\\nbypass it by crafting a malicious authorization request.\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"3\",\n      id: \"token-passthrough\",\n      children: \"Token Passthrough\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"“Token passthrough” is an anti-pattern where an MCP server accepts\\ntokens from an MCP client without validating that the tokens were\\nproperly issued \", _jsx(_components.em, {\n        children: \"to the MCP server\"\n      }), \" and passes them through to the\\ndownstream API.\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"risks\",\n      children: \"Risks\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"Token passthrough is explicitly forbidden in the\\n\", _jsx(_components.a, {\n        href: \"/specification/latest/basic/authorization\",\n        children: \"authorization specification\"\n      }), \"\\nas it introduces a number of security risks, that include:\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {\n          children: \"Security Control Circumvention\"\n        }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n          children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"The MCP Server or downstream APIs might implement important security\\ncontrols like rate limiting, request validation, or traffic\\nmonitoring, that depend on the token audience or other credential\\nconstraints. If clients can obtain and use tokens directly with the\\ndownstream APIs without the MCP server validating them properly or\\nensuring that the tokens are issued for the right service, they\\nbypass these controls.\"\n          }), \"\\n\"]\n        }), \"\\n\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {\n          children: \"Accountability and Audit Trail Issues\"\n        }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n          children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"The MCP Server will be unable to identify or distinguish between MCP\\nClients when clients are calling with an upstream-issued access token\\nwhich may be opaque to the MCP Server.\"\n          }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"The downstream Resource Server’s logs may show requests that appear\\nto come from a different source with a different identity, rather\\nthan the MCP server that is actually forwarding the tokens.\"\n          }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"Both factors make incident investigation, controls, and auditing\\nmore difficult.\"\n          }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"If the MCP Server passes tokens without validating their claims\\n(e.g., roles, privileges, or audience) or other metadata, a\\nmalicious actor in possession of a stolen token can use the server\\nas a proxy for data exfiltration.\"\n          }), \"\\n\"]\n        }), \"\\n\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {\n          children: \"Trust Boundary Issues\"\n        }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n          children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"The downstream Resource Server grants trust to specific entities.\\nThis trust might include assumptions about origin or client behavior\\npatterns. Breaking this trust boundary could lead to unexpected\\nissues.\"\n          }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"If the token is accepted by multiple services without proper\\nvalidation, an attacker compromising one service can use the token\\nto access other connected services.\"\n          }), \"\\n\"]\n        }), \"\\n\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {\n          children: \"Future Compatibility Risk\"\n        }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n          children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"Even if an MCP Server starts as a “pure proxy” today, it might need\\nto add security controls later. Starting with proper token audience\\nseparation makes it easier to evolve the security model.\"\n          }), \"\\n\"]\n        }), \"\\n\"]\n      }), \"\\n\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"mitigation-2\",\n      children: \"Mitigation\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"MCP servers \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"MUST NOT\"\n      }), \" accept any tokens that were not explicitly\\nissued for the MCP server.\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"3\",\n      id: services.\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"attack-description-2\",\n      children: \"Attack Description\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: for\\ndevelopment)\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"Link-local: \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"169.254.0.0/16\"\n        }), \" (including \"Session Hijacking\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: \"Session hijacking is an attack vector where a client is provided a\\nsession ID by the server, and an unauthorized party is able to obtain\\nand use that same session ID to impersonate the original client and\\nperform unauthorized actions on their behalf.\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"session-hijack-prompt-injection\",\n      children: \"Session Hijack Prompt Injection\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Mermaid, {\n      chart: \"sequenceDiagram\\n    participant Client\\n    participant ServerA\\n    participant Queue\\n    participant ServerB\\n    participant Attacker\\n\\n    Client-\u003e\u003eServerA: Initialize (connect to streamable HTTP server)\\n    ServerA--\u003e\u003eClient: Respond with session ID\\n\\n    Attacker-\u003e\u003eServerB: Access/guess session ID\\n    Note right of Attacker: Attacker knows/guesses session ID\\n\\n    Attacker-\u003e\u003eServerB: Trigger event (malicious payload, using session ID)\\n    ServerB-\u003e\u003eQueue: Enqueue event (keyed by session ID)\\n\\n    ServerA-\u003e\u003eQueue: Poll for events (using session ID)\\n    Queue--\u003e\u003eServerA: Event data (malicious payload)\\n\\n    ServerA--\u003e\u003eClient: Async response (malicious payload)\\n    Client-\u003e\u003eClient: Acts based on malicious payload\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"session-hijack-impersonation\",\n      children: \"Session Hijack Impersonation\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Mermaid, {\n      chart: \"sequenceDiagram\\n    participant Client\\n    participant Server\\n    participant Attacker\\n\\n    Client-\u003e\u003eServer: Initialize }), \" enqueues the event (associated with session ID) into a\\nshared queue.\"]\n        }), \"\\n\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n          children: [_jsx(_components.strong, {\n            children: \"Server A\"\n          }), \" polls the queue for events using the session ID and\\nretrieves the malicious payload.\"]\n _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"Session Hijack Impersonation\"\n      })\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ol, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"The MCP client authenticates with the MCP server, creating a\\npersistent session ID.\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"The MCP Servers \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"MUST NOT\"\n      }), \" use sessions for authentication.\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"MCP servers \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"MUST\"\n      }), \" use secure, non-deterministic session IDs.\\nGenerated session IDs (e.g., UUIDs) \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"SHOULD\"\n      }), \" use secure random number\\ngenerators. Avoid predictable or sequential session identifiers that\\ncould be guessed by an attacker. \"risks-3\",\n      children: \"Risks\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: \"Local MCP servers with inadequate restrictions or from untrusted sources\\nintroduce several critical children: \"Show the exact command that will be executed, without truncation\\n(include arguments and parameters)\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Clearly identify it as a potentially dangerous operation that executes\\ncode on the user’s system\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Require explicit user approval before proceeding\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Allow users to cancel the configuration\"\n      }), \"\\n\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"The MCP client \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"SHOULD\"\n      }), \" implement additional checks and guardrails to\\nmitigate potential code execution attack vectors:\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"Highlight potentially dangerous command patterns (e.g., commands\\ncontaining \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"sudo\"\n        }), \", \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"rm -rf\"\n        }), \", network operations, file system access\\noutside children: \"Execute MCP server commands in a sandboxed environment with minimal\\ndefault privileges\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Launch MCP servers with restricted access to the file system, network,\\nand other system resources\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Provide mechanisms for users to explicitly grant additional privileges\\n(e.g., specific directory access, network access) when needed\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Use platform-appropriate sandboxing technologies (containers, chroot,\\napplication sandboxes, etc.)\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Keep sandboxing solutions up-to-date to account for emerging\\nvulnerabilities\"\n      }), \"\\n\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"MCP servers intending for their servers to be run locally \", _jsx(_components.strong, {\n        children: \"SHOULD\"\n      }), \"\\nimplement measures to prevent unauthorized usage from malicious\\nprocesses:\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"Use the \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n          children: \"stdio\"\n        }), \" transport to limit access to just the MCP client\"]\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.li, {\n        children: [\"Restrict access if using an HTTP transport, such as:\", \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n          children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"Require an authorization token\"\n          }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n            children: \"Use unix domain sockets or other Interprocess Communication (IPC)\\nmechanisms with restricted access\"\n          }), \"\\n\"]\n        }), \"\\n\"]\n      }), \"\\n\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"3\",\n      id: \"scope-minimization\",\n      children: \"Scope Minimization\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.p, {\n      children: \"Poor scope design increases token compromise impact, elevates user\\nfriction, and obscures audit trails.\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"attack-description-5\",\n      children: \"Attack Description\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.p, {\n      children: [\"An attacker obtains (via log leakage, memory scraping, or local\\ninterception) an access token carrying broad scopes (\", _jsx(_components.code, {\n        children: \"files:*\"\n      }), \", \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n        children: \"db:*\"\n      }), \",\\n\", _jsx(_components.code, {\n        children: \"admin:*\"\n      }), \") that were granted up front because the MCP server exposed\\nevery scope in \", _jsx(_components.code, {\n        children: \"scopes_supported\"\n      }), \" and the client requested them all.\\nThe token enables lateral data access, privilege chaining, and difficult\\nrevocation without re-consenting the entire surface.\"]\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsx(Heading, {\n      level: \"4\",\n      id: \"risks-4\",\n      children: \"Risks\"\n    }), \"\\n\", _jsxs(_components.ul, {\n      children: [\"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Expanded blast radius: stolen broad token enables unrelated\\ntool/resource access\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Higher friction on revocation: revoking a max-privilege token disrupts\\nall workflows\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Audit noise: single omnibus scope masks user intent per operation\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Privilege chaining: attacker can immediately invoke high-risk tools\\nwithout further elevation prompts\"\n      }), \"\\n\", _jsx(_components.li, {\n        children: \"Consent abandonment: users decline dialogs listing excessive scopes\"\n      }), \"\\n\",
